ConfigAction {\n402\t    /// Initialize global config and data directory\n403\t    Init {\n404\t        /// Force reinitialization\n405\t        #[arg(long)]\n406\t        force: bool,\n407\t    },\n408\t    /// Show current configuration\n409\t    Show,\n410\t    /// Set a configuration value\n411\t    Set {\n412\t        /// Configuration key (e.g., general.log_level)\n413\t        key: String,\n414\t        /// Configuration value\n415\t        value: String,\n416\t    },\n417\t    /// Get a configuration value\n418\t    Get {\n419\t        /// Configuration key\n420\t        key: String,\n421\t    },\n422\t}\n423\t\n424\t/// Plugins subcommands\n425\t#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\n426\tenum PluginsAction {\n427\t    /// List available plugins\n428\t    List {\n429\t        /// subcommands\n446\t#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\n447\tenum IndexAction {\n448\t    /// Drop and rebuild the index from session files\n449\t    Rebuild {\n450\t        /// Only re-index sessions from this plugin\n451\t        #[arg(short, long)]\n452\t        plugin: Option<String>,\n453\t\n454\t        /// Tantivy writer heap size in MB\n455\t        #[arg(long, default_value = \"50\")]\n456\t        heap_size: usize,\n457\t    },\n458\t    /// Show index statistics\n459\t    Stats,\n460\t    /// Merge segments for better query performance\n461\t    Optimize,\n462\t}\n463\t\n464\t/// Daemon subcommands\n465\t#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\n466\tenum DaemonAction {\n467\t    /// Start the daemon in the background\n468\t    Start,\n469\t    /// Run the daemon in the foreground (for #[arg(long)]\n477\t        json: bool,\n478\t    },\n479\t    /// Tail the daemon log\n480\t    Logs {\n481\t        /// Follow mode (like tail -f)\n482\t        #[arg(short = 'f', long)]\n483\t        follow: bool,\n484\t\n485\t        /// Number of lines to show (default: 20)\n486\t        #[arg(short = 'n', long, default_value = \"20\")]\n487\t        lines: usize,\n488\t    },\n489\t    /// Install systemd user service unit (~/.config/systemd/user/agentscribe.service)\n490\t    Install,\n491\t    /// Remove systemd user service unit\n492\t    Uninstall,\n493\t}\n494\t\n495\t/// Table row for plugin list output\n496\t#[derive(Tabled)]\n497\tstruct PluginRow {\n498\t    name: String,\n499\t    version: String,\n500\t    format: String,\n501\t}\n502\t\n503\t/// Run the CLI\n504\tpub fn run() -> Result<()> {\n505\t    let args = Args::parse();\n506\t\n507\t    match args.command {\n508\t        Commands::Config { action } => run_config(action),\n509\t        Commands::Plugins { action } => run_plugins(action),\n510\t        Commands::Scrape {\n511\t            plugin,\n512\t            file,\n513\t            dry_run,\n514\t            output_events,\n515\t            json,\n516\t        } => run_scrape(plugin, file, dry_run, output_events, json),\n517\t        Commands::Status { json, plugin } => run_status(json, plugin),\n518\t        Commands::Index { action } => run_index(action),\n519\t        Commands::Search {\n520\t            query,\n521\t            error,\n522\t            code,\n523\t            lang,\n524\t            solution_only,\n525\t            like,\n526\t            session,\n527\t            agent,\n528\t            project,\n529\t            since,\n530\t            before,\n531\t            tag,\n532\t            outcome,\n533\t            r#type,\n534\t            model,\n535\t            fuzzy,\n536\t            edit_distance,\n537\t            max_results,\n538\t            snippet_length,\n539\t            token_budget,\n540\t            offset,\n541\t            sort,\n542\t            hint,\n543\t            json,\n544\t        } => run_search(\n545\t            query,\n546\t            error,\n547\t            code,\n548\t            lang,\n549\t            solution_only,\n550\t            like,\n551\t            session,\n552\t            agent,\n553\t            project,\n554\t            since,\n555\t            before,\n556\t            tag,\n557\t            outcome,\n558\t            r#type,\n559\t            model,\n560\t            fuzzy,\n561\t            edit_distance,\n562\t            max_results,\n563\t            snippet_length,\n564\t            token_budget,\n565\t            offset,\n566\t            sort,\n567\t            hint,\n568\t            json,\n569\t        ),\n570\t        Commands::Recurring {\n571\t            since,\n572\t            threshold,\n573\t            json,\n574\t        } => run_recurring(since, threshold, json),\n575\t        Commands::Daemon { action } => run_daemon(action),\n576\t        Commands::Rules {\n577\t            project_path,\n578\t            format,\n579\t            json,\n580\t        } => run_rules(project_path, format, json),\n581\t        Commands::Analytics {\n582\t            agent,\n583\t            project,\n584\t            since,\n585\t            json,\n586\t        } => run_analytics(agent, project, since, json),\n587\t        Commands::Gc {\n588\t            older_than,\n589\t            dry_run,\n590\t            json,\n591\t        } => run_gc(older_than, dry_run, json),\n592\t        Commands::Blame {\n593\t            spec,\n594\t            max_results,\n595\t            json,\n596\t        } => run_blame(spec, max_results, json),\n597\t        Commands::File {\n598\t            path,\n599\t            max_results,\n600\t            json,\n601\t        } => run_file(path, max_results, json),\n602\t        Commands::Summarize {\n603\t            session,\n604\t            since,\n605\t            project,\n606\t            max_results,\n607\t            write,\n608\t            json,\n609\t        } => run_summarize(session, since, project, max_results, write, json),\n610\t        Commands::ShellHook { shell } => run_shell_hook(&shell),\n611\t        Commands::FileKnowledge { file_path, json } => run_file_knowledge(&file_path, json),\n612\t        Commands::Digest {\n613\t            since,\n614\t            output,\n615\t            json,\n616\t        } => run_digest(since, output, json),\n617\t        Commands::PulseReport {\n618\t            quarter,\n619\t            output,\n620\t            format,\n621\t        } => run_pulse_report(quarter, output, format),\n622\t        Commands::Capacity {\n623\t            account_dir,\n624\t            cache_max_age,\n625\t            json,\n626\t        } => run_capacity(account_dir, cache_max_age, json),\n627\t        Commands::Transcribe {\n628\t            input,\n629\t            wait,\n630\t            timeout,\n631\t            json,\n632\t        } => run_transcribe(input, wait, timeout, json),\n633\t        Commands::Context {\n634\t            query,\n635\t cmd = Args::command();\n646\t            generate(shell, &mut cmd, \"agentscribe\", &mut io::stdout());\n647\t            Ok(())\n648\t        }\n649\t    }\n650\t}\n651\t\n652\t/// Run daemon commands\n653\tfn run_daemon(action: DaemonAction) -> Result<()> {\n654\t    // install/uninstall don't need the data directory to exist\n655\t    match action {\n656\t        DaemonAction::Install => return crate::daemon::install_service(),\n657\t        DaemonAction::Uninstall => return crate::daemon::uninstall_service(),\n658\t        _ => {}\n659\t    }\n660\t\n661\t    let config = load_config()?;\n662\t    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n663\t\n664\t    // Ensure data directory exists for all other daemon commands\n665\t    if !data_dir.exists() {\n666\t        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n667\t        std::process::exit(1);\n668\t    }\n669\t\n670\t    match action {\n671\t        DaemonAction::Start => {\n672\t            crate::daemon::start(&data_dir)?;\n673\t            Ok(())\n674\t        }\n675\t        DaemonAction::Run => crate::daemon::run(&data_dir),\n676\t        DaemonAction::Stop => crate::daemon::stop(&data_dir),\n677\t        DaemonAction::Status { json } => {\n678\t            let info = crate::daemon::status(&data_dir)?;\n679\t            if json {\n680\t                println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&info).unwrap());\n681\t            } else {\n682\t                print_daemon_status(&info);\n683\t            }\n684\t            Ok(())\n685\t        }\n686\t        DaemonAction::Logs { follow, lines } => crate::daemon::logs(&data_dir, follow, lines),\n687\t        // Already handled above\n688\t        DaemonAction::Install | DaemonAction::Uninstall => unreachable!(),\n689\t    }\n690\t}\n691\t\n692\t/// Format daemon status for human-readable output\n693\tfn print_daemon_status(info: &crate::daemon::DaemonInfo) {\n694\t    if !info.running {\n695\t        println!(\"Daemon: stopped\");\n696\t        return;\n697\t    }\n698\t\n699\t    println!(\"Daemon: running\");\n700\t\n701\t    if let Some(pid) = info.pid {\n702\t        println!(\"  PID: {}\", pid);\n703\t    }\n704\t\n705\t    if let Some(secs) = info.uptime_secs {\n706\t        println!(\"  Uptime: {}\", crate::daemon::format_duration(secs));\n707\t    }\n708\t\n709\t    if let Some(rss) = info.rss_bytes {\n710\t        println!(\"  RSS: {}\", crate::daemon::format_bytes(rss));\n711\t    }\n712\t\n713\t    if let Some(peak) = info.peak_rss_bytes {\n714\t        println!(\"  Peak RSS: {}\", crate::daemon::format_bytes(peak));\n715\t    }\n716\t\n717\t    if let Some(sessions) = info.sessions_indexed {\n718\t        println!(\"  Sessions indexed: {}\", sessions);\n719\t    }\n720\t\n721\t    if let Some(ts) = info.last_scrape {\n722\t        println!(\"  Last scrape: {}\", ts.to_rfc3339());\n723\t    }\n724\t\n725\t    if let Some(ts) = info.started_at {\n726\t        println!(\"  Started at: {}\", ts.to_rfc3339());\n727\t    }\n728\t}\n729\t\n730\t/// Run config commands\n731\tfn run_config(action: ConfigAction) -> Result<()> {\n732\t    match action {\n733\t        ConfigAction::Init { force } => {\n734\t            let data_dir = config::init(force)?;\n735\t            println!(\n736\t                \"Initialized AgentScribe data directory: {}\",\n737\t                data_dir.display()\n738\t            );\n739\t            Ok(())\n740\t        }\n741\t        ConfigAction::Show => {\n742\t            let config = load_config()?;\n743\t            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n744\t            println!(\"Data directory: {}\", data_dir.display());\n745\t            println!(\"Log level: {}\", config.general.log_level);\n746\t            println!(\"\\nScraping:\");\n747\t            println!(\"  Debounce: {}s\", config.scrape.debounce_seconds);\n748\t            println!(\n749\t                \"  Max session age: {} days\",\n750\t                config.scrape.max_session_age_days\n751\t            );\n752\t            println!(\"  Git auto-commit: {}\", config.scrape.git_auto_commit);\n753\t            println!(\"\\nSearch:\");\n754\t            println!(\n755\t                \"  Default max results: {}\",\n756\t                config.search.default_max_results\n757\t            );\n758\t            println!(\n759\t                \"  Default snippet length: {}\",\n760\t                config.search.default_snippet_length\n761\t            );\n762\t            Ok(())\n763\t        }\n764\t        ConfigAction::Set { key, value } => {\n765\t            let mut config = load_config()?;\n766\t            // Simple key-path setter (could be enhanced)\n767\t            match key.split('.').collect::<Vec<_>>().as_slice() {\n768\t                [\"general\", \"log_level\"] => config.general.log_level = value.clone(),\n769\t                [\"scrape\", \"debounce_seconds\"] => {\n770\t                    config.scrape.debounce_seconds = value.parse().unwrap_or(5);\n771\t                }\n772\t                [\"scrape\", \"max_session_age_days\"] => {\n773\t                    config.scrape.max_session_age_days = value.parse().unwrap_or(0);\n774\t                }\n775\t                [\"scrape\", \"git_auto_commit\"] => {\n776\t                    config.scrape.git_auto_commit =\n777\t                        matches!(value.to_lowercase().as_str(), \"true\" | \"1\" | \"yes\");\n778\t                }\n779\t                _ => {\n780\t                    eprintln!(\"Unknown configuration key: {}\", key);\n781\t                    return Ok(());\n782\t                }\n783\t            }\n784\t\n785\t            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n786\t            let config_path = data_dir.join(\"config.toml\");\n787\t            config.save(&config_path)?;\n788\t            println!(\"Set {} = {}\", key, value);\n789\t            Ok(())\n790\t        }\n791\t        ConfigAction::Get { key } => {\n792\t            let config = load_config()?;\n793\t            let value = match key.split('.').collect::<Vec<_>>().as_slice() {\n794\t                [\"general\", \"data_dir\"] => config.data_dir()?.display().to_string(),\n795\t                [\"general\", \"log_level\"] => config.general.log_level.clone(),\n796\t                [\"scrape\", \"debounce_seconds\"] => config.scrape.debounce_seconds.to_string(),\n797\t                [\"scrape\", \"max_session_age_days\"] => {\n798\t                    config.scrape.max_session_age_days.to_string()\n799\t                }\n800\t                [\"scrape\", \"git_auto_commit\"] => config.scrape.git_auto_commit.to_string(),\n801\t                _ => {\n802\t                    eprintln!(\"Unknown configuration key: {}\", key);\n803\t                    return Ok(());\n804\t                }\n805\t            };\n806\t            println!(\"{}\", value);\n807\t            Ok(())\n808\t        }\n809\t    }\n810\t}\n811\t\n812\t/// Run plugins commands\n813\tfn run_plugins(action: PluginsAction) -> Result<()> {\n814\t    match action {\n815\t        PluginsAction::List { verbose } => {\n816\t            let config = load_config()?;\n817\t            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n818\t            let plugin_dir = data_dir.join(\"plugins\");\n819\t\n820\t            let mut scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir)?;\n821\t            scraper.load_plugins()?;\n822\t\n823\t            let mut rows = Vec::new();\n824\t\n825\t            for (name, plugin) in scraper.plugin_manager().all() {\n826\t                rows.push(PluginRow {\n827\t                    name: name.clone(),\n828\t                    version: plugin.plugin.version.clone(),\n829\t                    format: plugin.source.format.as_str().to_string(),\n830\t                });\n831\t\n832\t                if verbose {\n833\t                    println!(\"Plugin: {}\", name);\n834\t                    println!(\"  Version: {}\", plugin.plugin.version);\n835\t                    println!(\"  Format: {}\", plugin.source.format.as_str());\n836\t                    println!(\"  Paths:\");\n837\t                    for path in &plugin.source.paths {\n838\t                        println!(\"    - {}\", path);\n839\t                    }\n840\t                    println!();\n841\t                }\n842\t            }\n843\t\n844\t            if !verbose {\n845\t                if rows.is_empty() {\n846\t                    println!(\"No plugins found in {}\", plugin_dir.display());\n847\t                } else {\n848\t                    println!(\"{}\", Table::new(rows));\n849\t                }\n850\t            }\n851\t\n852\t            Ok(())\n853\t        }\n854\t        PluginsAction::Validate { path } => {\n855\t            let plugin = validate_plugin_file(&path)?;\n856\t            println!(\"Plugin '{}' is valid!\", plugin.plugin.name);\n857\t            println!(\"  Version: {}\", plugin.plugin.version);\n858\t            println!(\"  Format: {}\", plugin.source.format.as_str());\n859\t            Ok(())\n860\t        }\n861\t        PluginsAction::Show { name } => {\n862\t            let config = load_config()?;\n863\t            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n864\t            let mut scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir)?;\n865\t            scraper.load_plugins()?;\n866\t\n867\t            if let Some(plugin) = scraper.plugin_manager().get(&name) {\n868\t                println!(\"Plugin: {}\", plugin.plugin.name);\n869\t                println!(\"  Version: {}\", plugin.plugin.version);\n870\t                println!(\"  Format: {}\", plugin.source.format.as_str());\n871\t                println!(\"\\n  Source paths:\");\n872\t                for path in &plugin.source.paths {\n873\t                    println!(\"    - {}\", path);\n874\t                }\n875\t                if !plugin.source.exclude.is_empty() {\n876\t                    println!(\"  Excludes:\");\n877\t                    for pattern in &plugin.source.exclude {\n878\t                        println!(\"    - {}\", pattern);\n879\t                    }\n880\t                }\n881\t                println!(\"\\n  Session detection:\");\n882\t                match &plugin.source.session_detection {\n883\t                    crate::plugin::SessionDetection::OneFilePerSession { .. } => {\n884\t                        println!(\"    Method: one-file-per-session\");\n885\t                    }\n886\t                    crate::plugin::SessionDetection::TimestampGap { gap_threshold } => {\n887\t                        println!(\"    Method: timestamp-gap ({})\", gap_threshold);\n888\t                    }\n889\t                    crate::plugin::SessionDetection::Delimiter { delimiter_pattern } => {\n890\t                        println!(\"    Method: delimiter ({})\", delimiter_pattern);\n891\t                    }\n892\t                }\n893\t            } else {\n894\t                eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", name);\n895\t                std::process::exit(1);\n896\t            }\n897\t\n898\t            Ok(())\n899\t        }\n900\t    }\n901\t}\n902\t\n903\t/// Run scrape command\n904\tfn run_scrape(\n905\t    plugin: Option<String>,\n906\t    file: Option<PathBuf>,\n907\t    dry_run: bool,\n908\t    _output_events: bool,\n909\t    _json: bool,\n910\t) -> Result<()> {\n911\t    let config = load_config()?;\n912\t    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n913\t\n914\t    // Initialize if needed\n915\t    if !data_dir.exists() {\n916\t        println!(\"Data directory not found. Initializing...\");\n917\t        config::init(false)?;\n918\t    }\n919\t\n920\t    let mut scraper =\n921\t        Scraper::new_with_lock_timeout(data_dir.clone(), config.scrape.lock_timeout_seconds)?;\n922\t    scraper.load_plugins()?;\n923\t\n924\t    if let Some(file_path) = file {\n925\t        // Scrape single file\n926\t        println!(\"Scraping file: {}\", file_path.display());\n927\t\n928\t        // Determine plugin from file or use specified\n929\t        let plugin_name = plugin.clone().unwrap_or_else(|| {\n930\t            // Try to detect from file location\n931\t            let path_str = file_path.display().to_string();\n932\t            if path_str.contains(\".claude\") {\n933\t                \"claude-code\".to_string()\n934\t            } else if path_str.contains(\"aider\") {\n935\t                \"aider\".to_string()\n936\t            } else if path_str.contains(\"codex\") {\n937\t                \"codex\".to_string()\n938\t            } else if path_str.contains(\"opencode\") {\n939\t                \"opencode\".to_string()\n940\t            } else {\n941\t                eprintln!(\"Cannot auto-detect plugin. Use --plugin to specify.\");\n942\t                std::process::exit(1);\n943\t            }\n944\t        });\n945\t\n946\t        if let Some(p) = scraper.plugin_manager().get(&plugin_name).cloned() {\n947\t            if dry_run {\n948\t                println!(\"Dry run - would scrape with plugin: {}\", plugin_name);\n949\t                println!(\"  File: {}\", file_path.display());\n950\t                println!(\"  Format: {}\", p.source.format.as_str());\n951\t                // For dry run, just show we'd process it\n952\t                println!(\"  Would detect sessions and parse events...\");\n953\t            } else {\n954\t                let result = scraper.scrape_file(&file_path, &p)?;\n955\t                scraper.state_manager().save()?;\n956\t                println!(\"Scraped {} session(s)\", result.sessions_scraped);\n957\t                if result.sessions_indexed > 0 {\n958\t                    println!(\"Indexed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_indexed);\n959\t                }\n960\t                if !result.errors.is_empty() {\n961\t                    eprintln!(\"Errors: {}\", result.errors.len());\n962\t                }\n963\t                if config.scrape.git_auto_commit && git_auto_commit(&data_dir, &result)? {\n964\t                    println!(\"Git: committed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_scraped);\n965\t                }\n966\t            }\n967\t        } else {\n968\t            eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", plugin_name);\n969\t            std::process::exit(1);\n970\t        }\n971\t    } else if let Some(plugin_name) = plugin {\n972\t        // Scrape specific plugin\n973\t        println!(\"Scraping plugin: {}\", plugin_name);\n974\t\n975\t        if let Some(p) = scraper.plugin_manager().get(&plugin_name).cloned() {\n976\t            if dry_run {\n977\t                println!(\"Dry run - would discover and scrape files:\");\n978\t                let files = scraper.discover_files(&p)?;\n979\t                for file in files {\n980\t                    println!(\"  - {}\", file.display());\n981\t                }\n982\t            } else {\n983\t                let result = scraper.scrape_plugin(&p)?;\n984\t                scraper.state_manager().save()?;\n985\t                println!(\n986\t                    \"Scraped {} session(s) from {} file(s)\",\n987\t                    result.sessions_scraped, result.files_processed\n988\t                );\n989\t                if result.sessions_indexed > 0 {\n990\t                    println!(\"Indexed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_indexed);\n991\t                }\n992\t                if result.files_skipped > 0 {\n993\t                    println!(\"  ({} files unchanged, skipped)\", result.files_skipped);\n994\t                }\n995\t                if !result.errors.is_empty() {\n996\t                    eprintln!(\"Errors: {}\", result.errors.len());\n997\t                    for error in &result.errors[..result.errors.len().min(5)] {\n998\t                        eprintln!(\"  - {}: {}\", error.file, error.message);\n999\t                    }\n1000\t                    if result.errors.len() > 5 {\n1001\t                        eprintln!(\"  ... and {} more\", result.errors.len() - 5);\n1002\t                    }\n1003\t                }\n1004\t                if config.scrape.git_auto_commit && git_auto_commit(&data_dir, &result)? {\n1005\t                    println!(\"Git: committed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_scraped);\n1006\t                }\n1007\t            }\n1008\t        } else {\n1009\t            eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", plugin_name);\n1010\t            std::process::exit(1);\n1011\t        }\n1012\t    } else {\n1013\t        // Scrape all plugins\n1014\t        println!(\"Scraping all plugins...\");\n1015\t\n1016\t        if dry_run      total_docs, total_errors\n1298\t    );\n1299\t    Ok(())\n1300\t}\n1301\t\n1302\t/// Show index statistics.\n1303\tfn run_index_stats(data_dir: &std::path::Path) -> Result<()> {\n1304\t    let DaemonAction::Uninstall => return crate::daemon::uninstall_service(),\n        _ => {}\n    }\n\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    // Ensure data above\n        DaemonAction::Install | DaemonAction::Uninstall => unreachable!(),\n    }\n}\n\n/// Format daemon status for human-readable output\nfn print_daemon_status(info: &crate::daemon::DaemonInfo) {\n    if !info.running {\n        println!(\"Daemon: stopped\");\n        return;\n    }\n\n    println!(\"Daemon: running\");\n\n    if let Some(pid) = info.pid {\n info.rss_bytes {\n        println!(\"  RSS: {}\", crate::daemon::format_bytes(rss));\n    }\n\n    if let Some(peak) = info.peak_rss_bytes {\n        println!(\"  Peak RSS: {}\", crate::daemon::format_bytes(peak));\n    }\n\n    if let Some(sessions) = info.sessions_indexed {\n        println!(\"  Sessions indexed: {}\", sessions);\n    }\n\n    if let Some(ts) = }\n}\n\n/// Run config commands\nfn run_config(action: ConfigAction) -> Result<()> {\n    match action {\n        ConfigAction::Init { force } => {\n            let data_dir = config::init(force)?;\n \"log_level\"] => config.general.log_level = value.clone(),\n                [\"scrape\", \"debounce_seconds\"] => {\n                    config.scrape.debounce_seconds = value.parse().unwrap_or(5);\n                }\n                [\"scrape\", \"max_session_age_days\"] => {\n                    config.scrape.max_session_age_days = value.parse().unwrap_or(0);\n                }\n                [\"scrape\", \"git_auto_commit\"] => {\n                    config.scrape.git_auto_commit =\n                        matches!(value.to_lowercase().as_str(), \"true\" | \"1\" | \"yes\");\n                }\n                _ => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Unknown configuration key: {}\", key);\n                    return Ok(());\n                }\n            }\n\n            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n            let config_path = data_dir.join(\"config.toml\");\n            config.save(&config_path)?;\n            println!(\"Set {} = {}\", key, value);\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        ConfigAction::Get { key } => {\n            let config = load_config()?;\n            let value = match key.split('.').collect::<Vec<_>>().as_slice() {\n                [\"general\", \"data_dir\"] => config.data_dir()?.display().to_string(),\n                [\"general\", \"log_level\"] => config.general.log_level.clone(),\n                [\"scrape\", \"debounce_seconds\"] => config.scrape.debounce_seconds.to_string(),\n                [\"scrape\", \"max_session_age_days\"] => {\n                    config.scrape.max_session_age_days.to_string()\n                }\n                [\"scrape\", \"git_auto_commit\"] => config.scrape.git_auto_commit.to_string(),\n                _ => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Unknown configuration key: {}\", key);\n                    return Ok(());\n                }\n            };\n            println!(\"{}\", value);\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run plugins commands\nfn run_plugins(action: PluginsAction) -> Result<()> {\n    match action {\n        PluginsAction::List { verbose } => {\n            let config = load_config()?;\n            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n            let plugin_dir = data_dir.join(\"plugins\");\n\n            let mut scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir)?;\n            scraper.load_plugins()?;\n\n            let mut rows = Vec::new();\n\n            for (name, plugin) in scraper.plugin_manager().all() {\n                rows.push(PluginRow {\n                    name: name.clone(),\n                    version: plugin.plugin.version.clone(),\n                    format: plugin.source.format.as_str().to_string(),\n                });\n\n                if verbose {\n                    println!(\"Plugin: {}\", name);\n                    println!(\"  Version: {}\", plugin.plugin.version);\n                    println!(\"  Format: {}\", plugin.source.format.as_str());\n                    println!(\"  Paths:\");\n                    for path in &plugin.source.paths {\n                        println!(\"    - {}\", path);\n                    }\n                    println!();\n                }\n            }\n\n            if !verbose {\n                if rows.is_empty() {\n                    println!(\"No plugins found in {}\", plugin_dir.display());\n                } else {\n                    println!(\"{}\", Table::new(rows));\n                }\n            }\n\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        PluginsAction::Validate { path } => {\n            let plugin = validate_plugin_file(&path)?;\n            println!(\"Plugin '{}' is valid!\", plugin.plugin.name);\n            println!(\"  Version: {}\", plugin.plugin.version);\n            println!(\"  Format: {}\", plugin.source.format.as_str());\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        PluginsAction::Show { name } => {\n            let config = load_config()?;\n            let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n            let mut scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir)?;\n            scraper.load_plugins()?;\n\n            if let Some(plugin) = scraper.plugin_manager().get(&name) {\n                println!(\"Plugin: {}\", plugin.plugin.name);\n                println!(\"  Version: {}\", plugin.plugin.version);\n                println!(\"  Format: {}\", plugin.source.format.as_str());\n                println!(\"\\n  Source paths:\");\n                for path in &plugin.source.paths {\n                    println!(\"    - {}\", path);\n                }\n                if !plugin.source.exclude.is_empty() {\n                    println!(\"  Excludes:\");\n                    for pattern in &plugin.source.exclude {\n                        println!(\"    - {}\", pattern);\n                    }\n                }\n                println!(\"\\n  Session detection:\");\n                match &plugin.source.session_detection {\n                    crate::plugin::SessionDetection::OneFilePerSession { .. } => {\n                        println!(\"    Method: one-file-per-session\");\n                    }\n                    crate::plugin::SessionDetection::TimestampGap { gap_threshold } => {\n                        println!(\"    Method: timestamp-gap ({})\", gap_threshold);\n                    }\n                    crate::plugin::SessionDetection::Delimiter { delimiter_pattern } => {\n                        println!(\"    Method: delimiter ({})\", delimiter_pattern);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", name);\n                std::process::exit(1);\n            }\n\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run scrape command\nfn run_scrape(\n    plugin: Option<String>,\n    file: Option<PathBuf>,\n    dry_run: bool,\n    _output_events: bool,\n    _json: bool,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    // Initialize if needed\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        println!(\"Data directory not found. Initializing...\");\n        config::init(false)?;\n    }\n\n    let mut scraper =\n        Scraper::new_with_lock_timeout(data_dir.clone(), config.scrape.lock_timeout_seconds)?;\n    scraper.load_plugins()?;\n\n    if let Some(file_path) = file {\n        // Scrape single file\n        println!(\"Scraping file: {}\", file_path.display());\n\n        // Determine plugin from file or use specified\n        let plugin_name = plugin.clone().unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            // Try to detect from file location\n            let path_str = file_path.display().to_string();\n            if path_str.contains(\".claude\") {\n                \"claude-code\".to_string()\n            } else if path_str.contains(\"aider\") {\n                \"aider\".to_string()\n            } else if path_str.contains(\"codex\") {\n                \"codex\".to_string()\n            } else if path_str.contains(\"opencode\") {\n                \"opencode\".to_string()\n            } else {\n                eprintln!(\"Cannot auto-detect plugin. Use --plugin to specify.\");\n                std::process::exit(1);\n            }\n        });\n\n        if let Some(p) = scraper.plugin_manager().get(&plugin_name).cloned() {\n            if dry_run {\n                println!(\"Dry run - would scrape with plugin: {}\", plugin_name);\n                println!(\"  File: {}\", file_path.display());\n                println!(\"  Format: {}\", p.source.format.as_str());\n                // For dry run, just show we'd process it\n                println!(\"  Would detect sessions and parse events...\");\n            } else {\n                let result = scraper.scrape_file(&file_path, &p)?;\n                scraper.state_manager().save()?;\n                println!(\"Scraped {} session(s)\", result.sessions_scraped);\n                if result.sessions_indexed > 0 {\n                    println!(\"Indexed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_indexed);\n                }\n                if !result.errors.is_empty() {\n                    eprintln!(\"Errors: {}\", result.errors.len());\n                }\n                if config.scrape.git_auto_commit && git_auto_commit(&data_dir, &result)? {\n                    println!(\"Git: committed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_scraped);\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", plugin_name);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    } else if let Some(plugin_name) = plugin {\n        // Scrape specific plugin\n        println!(\"Scraping plugin: {}\", plugin_name);\n\n        if let Some(p) = scraper.plugin_manager().get(&plugin_name).cloned() {\n            if dry_run {\n                println!(\"Dry run - would discover and scrape files:\");\n                let files = scraper.discover_files(&p)?;\n                for file in files {\n                    println!(\"  - {}\", file.display());\n                }\n            } else {\n                let result = scraper.scrape_plugin(&p)?;\n                scraper.state_manager().save()?;\n                println!(\n                    \"Scraped {} session(s) from {} file(s)\",\n                    result.sessions_scraped, result.files_processed\n                );\n                if result.sessions_indexed > 0 {\n                    println!(\"Indexed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_indexed);\n                }\n                if result.files_skipped > 0 {\n                    println!(\"  ({} files unchanged, skipped)\", result.files_skipped);\n                }\n                if !result.errors.is_empty() {\n                    eprintln!(\"Errors: {}\", result.errors.len());\n                    for error in &result.errors[..result.errors.len().min(5)] {\n                        eprintln!(\"  - {}: {}\", error.file, error.message);\n                    }\n                    if result.errors.len() > 5 {\n                        eprintln!(\"  ... and {} more\", result.errors.len() - 5);\n                    }\n                }\n                if config.scrape.git_auto_commit && git_auto_commit(&data_dir, &result)? {\n                    println!(\"Git: committed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_scraped);\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", plugin_name);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Scrape all plugins\n        println!(\"Scraping all plugins...\");\n\n        if dry_run {\n            for plugin_name in scraper.plugin_manager().names() {\n                println!(\"  - {}\", plugin_name);\n            }\n        } else {\n            let result = scraper.scrape_all()?;\n            println!(\"Scraped {} session(s) total\", result.sessions_scraped);\n            if result.sessions_indexed > 0 {\n                println!(\"Indexed {} session(s)\", result.sessions_indexed);\n            }\n            if !result.errors.is_empty() {\n                eprintln!(\"Errors: {}\", result.errors.len());\n            }\n            if config.scrape.git_auto_commit && git_auto_commit(&data_dir, &result)? {\n                println!(\n                    \"Git: committed {} session(s) ({})\",\n                    result.sessions_scraped,\n                    result.agent_types.join(\", \")\n                );\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run search command\n#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]\nfn run_search(\n    query: Option<String>,\n    error: Option<String>,\n    code: Option<String>,\n    lang: Option<String>,\n    solution_only: bool,\n    like: Option<String>,\n    session: Option<String>,\n    agent: Vec<String>,\n    project: Option<String>,\n    since: Option<String>,\n    before: Option<String>,\n    tag: Vec<String>,\n    outcome: Option<String>,\n    doc_type_filter: Option<String>,\n    model: Option<String>,\n    fuzzy: bool,\n    edit_distance: Option<u8>,\n    max_results: usize,\n    snippet_length: usize,\n    token_budget: Option<usize>,\n    offset: usize,\n    sort: String,\n    hint: bool,\n    json: bool,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    let sort_order = match sort.as_str() {\n        \"newest\" => SortOrder::Newest,\n        \"oldest\" => SortOrder::Oldest,\n        \"turns\" => SortOrder::Turns,\n        _ => SortOrder::Relevance,\n    };\n\n    let since_dt = since.as_deref().map(search::parse_datetime).transpose()?;\n\n    let before_dt = before.as_deref().map(search::parse_datetime).transpose()?;\n\n    let opts = SearchOptions {\n        query,\n        error_pattern: error,\n        code_query: code,\n        code_lang: lang,\n        solution_only,\n        like_session: like,\n        session_id: session,\n        agent,\n        project,\n        since: since_dt,\n        before: before_dt,\n        tag,\n        outcome,\n        doc_type_filter,\n        model,\n        file_path: None,\n        git_commit: None,\n        fuzzy,\n        fuzzy_distance: edit_distance.unwrap_or(config.search.fuzzy_edit_distance),\n        max_results,\n        snippet_length,\n        token_budget,\n        offset,\n        sort: sort_order,\n    };\n\n    let output = search::execute_search(&data_dir, &opts)?;\n\n    if hint {\n        // Print a single-line hint for shell hook integration\n        if let Some(result) = output.results.first() {\n            let text = result\n                .snippet\n                .as_deref()\n                .or(result.summary.as_deref())\n                .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                .trim();\n            let one_line: String = text.split_whitespace().collect::<Vec<_>>().join(\" \");\n            if !one_line.is_empty() {\n                if one_line.len() > 120 {\n                    println!(\"{}...\", &one_line[..117]);\n                } else {\n                    println!(\"{}\", one_line);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    } else if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        println!(\"{}\", search::format_human(&output, snippet_length));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run shell-hook command\nfn run_shell_hook(shell: &str) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config().unwrap_or_default();\n    let snippet = crate::shell_hook::generate_hook(shell, &config.shell_hook)?;\n    print!(\"{}\", snippet);\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run index subcommands\nfn run_index(action: IndexAction) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    match action {\n        IndexAction::Rebuild { plugin, heap_size } => {\n            run_index_rebuild(&data_dir, plugin.as_deref(), heap_size)\n        }\n        IndexAction::Stats => run_index_stats(&data_dir),\n        IndexAction::Optimize => run_index_optimize(&data_dir),\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run index rebuild: drop existing index and rebuild from session files.\nfn run_index_rebuild(\n    data_dir: &std::path::Path,\n    plugin_filter: Option<&str>,\n    heap_size: usize,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n\n    if !sessions_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"No sessions directory found. Run 'agentscribe scrape' first.\");\n        std::process::exit(2);\n    }\n\n    // Drop existing index\n    let index_path = data_dir.join(\"index\").join(\"tantivy\");\n    if index_path.exists() {\n        println!(\"Dropping existing index...\");\n        std::fs::remove_dir_all(&index_path)?;\n    }\n\n    let mut manager = IndexManager::open(data_dir)?;\n    manager.set_heap_size(heap_size);\n    manager.begin_write()?;\n\n    let mut total_docs = 0usize;\n    let mut total_errors = 0usize;\n\n    // Walk session directories\n    let entries = match std::fs::read_dir(&sessions_dir) {\n        Ok(e) => e,\n        Err(_) => {\n            eprintln!(\"Cannot read sessions directory.\");\n            std::process::exit(2);\n        }\n    };\n\n    for agent_entry in entries.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n        let agent_path = agent_entry.path();\n        if !agent_path.is_dir() {\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        let agent_name = match agent_path.file_name().and_then(|n| n.to_str()) {\n            Some(n) => n.to_string(),\n            None => continue,\n        };\n\n        // Apply plugin filter\n        if let Some(filter) = plugin_filter {\n            if agent_name != filter {\n                continue;\n            }\n        }\n\n        let session_files = match std::fs::read_dir(&agent_path) {\n            Ok(e) => e,\n            Err(_) => continue,\n        };\n\n        for session_entry in session_files.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n            let session_path = session_entry.path();\n            if session_path.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()) != Some(\"jsonl\") {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            let session_id = format!(\n                \"{}/{}\",\n                agent_name,\n                session_path\n                    .file_stem()\n                    .and_then(|s| s.to_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"unknown\")\n            );\n\n            // Read events from the normalized session file\n            let file = match std::fs::File::open(&session_path) {\n                Ok(f) => f,\n                Err(e) => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Error reading {}: {}\", session_path.display(), e);\n                    total_errors += 1;\n                    continue;\n                }\n            };\n\n            use std::io::BufRead;\n            let reader = std::io::BufReader::new(file);\n            let mut events = Vec::new();\n\n            for line in reader.lines() {\n                match line {\n                    Ok(l) => {\n                        if let Ok(event) = crate::event::Event::from_jsonl(&l) {\n                            events.push(event);\n                        }\n                    }\n                    Err(_) => {\n                        total_errors += 1;\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            if events.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Build manifest from events\n            let first = &events[0];\n            let manifest = crate::index::build_manifest_from_events(\n                &events,\n                &session_id,\n                &agent_name,\n                first.project.as_deref(),\n                first.model.as_deref(),\n            );\n\n            match manager.index_session(&events, &manifest) {\n                Ok(_) => total_docs += 1,\n                Err(e) => {\n                    eprintln!(\"Error indexing {}: {}\", session_id, e);\n                    total_errors += 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    manager.finish()?;\n\n    println!(\n        \"Rebuilt index from {} session files ({} errors)\",\n        total_docs, total_errors\n    );\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Show index statistics.\nfn run_index_stats(data_dir: &std::path::Path) -> Result<()> {\n    let index_path = data_dir.join(\"index\").join(\"tantivy\");\n\n    if !index_path.exists() {\n        println!(\"Index not found. Run 'agentscribe scrape' first.\");\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    let index = match search::open_index(data_dir) {\n        Ok(i) => i,\n        Err(e) => {\n            eprintln!(\"Error opening index: {}\", e);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    let reader = index.reader().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Failed to create reader: {}\", e))\n    })?;\n    let searcher = reader.searcher();\n\n    let num_docs = searcher.num_docs();\n    let segments = index.searchable_segment_metas().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Failed to get segment metas: {}\", e))\n    })?;\n    let num_segments = segments.len();\n    let schema = index.schema();\n    let fields: Vec<String> = schema\n        .fields()\n        .map(|(field, _)| schema.get_field_name(field).to_string())\n        .collect();\n\n    let size_bytes = dir_size(&index_path);\n\n    println!(\"Tantivy index at {}\", index_path.display());\n    println!(\"  Documents:    {}\", num_docs);\n    println!(\"  Segments:     {}\", num_segments);\n    println!(\"  Size on disk: {}\", format_bytes(size_bytes));\n    println!(\"  Fields:       {}\", fields.join(\", \"));\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Optimize the index by merging segments.\nfn run_index_optimize(data_dir: &std::path::Path) -> Result<()> {\n    let index_path = data_dir.join(\"index\").join(\"tantivy\");\n\n    if !index_path.exists() {\n        println!(\"Index not found. Run 'agentscribe scrape' first.\");\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    let pre_size = dir_size(&index_path);\n\n    let index = search::open_index(data_dir)?;\n    let segment_ids = index.searchable_segment_ids().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Failed to get segment IDs: {}\", e))\n    })?;\n    let num_segments = segment_ids.len();\n\n    println!(\"Merging {} segments...\", num_segments);\n\n    let mut writer = index\n        .writer::<tantivy::TantivyDocument>(50_000_000)\n        .map_err(|e| {\n            crate::error::AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Failed to open writer: {}\", e))\n        })?;\n\n    // Merge all segments into one and wait for completion\n    writer.merge(&segment_ids).wait().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Failed to merge segments: {}\", e))\n    })?;\n    writer.garbage_collect_files().wait().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Failed to garbage collect: {}\", e))\n    })?;\n\n    let post_size = dir_size(&index_path);\n\n    println!(\n        \"Merged {} segments ({} → {})\",\n        num_segments,\n        format_bytes(pre_size),\n        format_bytes(post_size)\n    );\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run status command\nfn run_status(json: bool, plugin_filter: Option<String>) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n    let data_dir_str = data_dir.display().to_string();\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let mut scraper = Scraper::new(data_dir.clone())?;\n    scraper.load_plugins()?;\n\n    // Determine which plugins to show\n    let plugin_names: Vec<String> = if let Some(ref filter) = plugin_filter {\n        if scraper.plugin_manager().get(filter).is_some() {\n            vec![filter.clone()]\n        } else {\n            eprintln!(\"Plugin '{}' not found\", filter);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    } else {\n        scraper\n            .plugin_manager()\n            .names()\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(String::from)\n            .collect()\n    };\n\n    // Gather scrape state\n    let scrape_state = scraper.state_manager().get_all();\n\n    // Collect per-plugin status\n    let mut plugin_statuses = Vec::new();\n    let mut _total_events: u64 = 0;\n    let mut total_sources: usize = 0;\n    let mut total_bytes: u64 = 0;\n\n    for plugin_name in &plugin_names {\n        let sessions = scraper.list_sessions(plugin_name)?;\n\n        // Count events across all sessions for this plugin\n        let mut plugin_events: u64 = 0;\n        for session_id in &sessions {\n            if let Ok(events) = scraper.read_session(session_id) {\n                plugin_events += events.len() as u64;\n            }\n        }\n        _total_events += plugin_events;\n\n        // Get source paths and truncation_limit from plugin config\n        let (source_paths, truncation_limit) = scraper\n            .plugin_manager()\n            .get(plugin_name)\n            .map(|p| (p.source.paths.clone(), p.source.truncation_limit))\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        // Find last scraped time and byte totals from scrape state for this plugin\n        let plugin_files: Vec<_> = scrape_state\n            .sources\n            .iter()\n            .filter(|(_, s)| s.plugin == *plugin_name)\n            .collect();\n\n        let last_scraped = plugin_files.iter().map(|(_, s)| s.last_scraped).max();\n\n        let mut plugin_bytes: u64 = 0;\n        for (_, file_state) in &plugin_files {\n            plugin_bytes += file_state.last_byte_offset;\n            total_bytes += file_state.last_byte_offset;\n        }\n        total_sources += plugin_files.len();\n\n        plugin_statuses.push(PluginStatus {\n            name: plugin_name.to_string(),\n            sessions: sessions.len(),\n            events: plugin_events,\n            last_scraped,\n            source_paths,\n            source_files: plugin_files.len(),\n            bytes: plugin_bytes,\n            truncation_limit,\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Daemon state (Phase 4 - check PID file if it exists)\n    let daemon_status = get_daemon_status(&data_dir);\n\n    // Disk usage of data directory\n    let dir_bytes = dir_size(&data_dir);\n\n    // Index stats (Phase 2 - check if index directory exists)\n    let index_dir = data_dir.join(\"index\");\n    let index_stats = get_index_stats(&index_dir);\n\n    if json {\n        use serde_json::json;\n        let mut plugins_json = Vec::new();\n        for ps in &plugin_statuses {\n            let mut p = json!({\n                \"name\": ps.name,\n                \"sessions\": ps.sessions,\n                \"events\": ps.events,\n                \"source_files\": ps.source_files,\n                \"bytes\": ps.bytes,\n                \"source_paths\": ps.source_paths,\n            });\n            if let Some(ts) = ps.last_scraped {\n                p[\"last_scraped\"] = json!(ts.to_rfc3339());\n            } else {\n                p[\"last_scraped\"] = json!(null);\n            }\n            plugins_json.push(p);\n        }\n\n        let status = json!({\n            \"version\": env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\"),\n            \"data_dir\": data_dir_str,\n            \"data_dir_bytes\": dir_bytes,\n            \"plugins\": plugins_json,\n            \"scrape_state\": {\n                \"tracked_sources\": total_sources,\n                \"total_bytes\": total_bytes,\n            },\n            \"daemon\": {\n                \"running\": daemon_status.running,\n                \"pid\": daemon_status.pid,\n            },\n            \"index\": {\n                \"exists\": index_stats.exists,\n                \"documents\": index_stats.documents,\n                \"size_bytes\": index_stats.size_bytes,\n            },\n        });\n\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&status).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        println!(\"AgentScribe v{}\", env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\"));\n        println!(\"Data dir: {} ({})\", data_dir_str, format_bytes(dir_bytes));\n\n        // Daemon\n        if daemon_status.running {\n            if let Some(pid) = daemon_status.pid {\n                println!(\"Daemon: running (PID {})\", pid);\n            } else {\n                println!(\"Daemon: running\");\n            }\n        } else {\n            println!(\"Daemon: stopped\");\n        }\n\n        // Plugins\n        println!(\"\\nPlugins:\");\n        if plugin_statuses.is_empty() {\n            println!(\"  (none)\");\n        }\n        for ps in &plugin_statuses {\n            let last = match ps.last_scraped {\n                Some(ts) => format_ago(ts),\n                None => \"never scraped\".to_string(),\n            };\n            println!(\n                \"  {:<14} {:>4} sessions  {:>6} events  {}  ({} source files, {})\",\n                ps.name,\n                ps.sessions,\n                ps.events,\n                last,\n                ps.source_files,\n                format_bytes(ps.bytes)\n            );\n        }\n\n        // Windsurf truncation warning\n        for ps in &plugin_statuses {\n            if ps.name == \"windsurf\" {\n                if let Some(limit) = ps.truncation_limit {\n                    println!(\n                        \"\\n  WARNING: Windsurf retains at most {} conversations.\",\n                        limit\n                    );\n                    println!(\n                        \"  Old conversations are silently overwritten. Run 'agentscribe scrape'\"\n                    );\n                    println!(\n                        \"  frequently (e.g., via 'agentscribe daemon start') to avoid data loss.\"\n                    );\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Index\n        if index_stats.exists {\n            println!(\n                \"\\nIndex: {} documents, {} on disk\",\n                index_stats.documents,\n                format_bytes(index_stats.size_bytes)\n            );\n        } else {\n            println!(\"\\nIndex: not built (run 'agentscribe index rebuild')\");\n        }\n\n        // Scrape state\n        println!(\n            \"\\nScrape state: tracking offsets for {} source paths ({} total)\",\n            total_sources,\n            format_bytes(total_bytes)\n        );\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Per-plugin status data\nstruct PluginStatus {\n    name: String,\n    sessions: usize,\n    events: u64,\n    last_scraped: Option<chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>>,\n    source_paths: Vec<String>,\n    source_files: usize,\n    bytes: u64,\n    truncation_limit: Option<u32>,\n}\n\n/// Daemon status info\nstruct DaemonStatus {\n    running: bool,\n    pid: Option<u32>,\n}\n\n/// Index stats\nstruct IndexStats {\n    exists: bool,\n    documents: usize,\n    size_bytes: u64,\n}\n\n/// Check daemon status by reading PID file\nfn get_daemon_status(data_dir: &std::path::Path) -> DaemonStatus {\n    let pid_file = data_dir.join(\"agentscribe.pid\");\n    if let Ok(content) = std::fs::read_to_string(&pid_file) {\n        if let Ok(pid) = content.trim().parse::<u32>() {\n            // Check if process is actually running\n            unsafe {\n                // kill(pid, 0) checks if process exists without sending a signal\n                if libc::kill(pid as i32, 0) == 0 {\n                    return DaemonStatus {\n                        running: true,\n                        pid: Some(pid),\n                    };\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    DaemonStatus {\n        running: false,\n        pid: None,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Get index stats\nfn get_index_stats(index_dir: &std::path::Path) -> IndexStats {\n    let tantivy_dir = index_dir.join(\"tantivy\");\n    if !tantivy_dir.exists() {\n        return IndexStats {\n            exists: false,\n            documents: 0,\n            size_bytes: 0,\n        };\n    }\n\n    let size_bytes = dir_size(&tantivy_dir);\n\n    // Read actual document count from Tantivy index\n    let documents = match tantivy::Index::open_in_dir(&tantivy_dir) {\n        Ok(index) => match index.reader() {\n            Ok(reader) => reader.searcher().num_docs() as usize,\n            Err(_) => 0,\n        },\n        Err(_) => 0,\n    };\n\n    IndexStats {\n        exists: documents > 0 || size_bytes > 0,\n        documents,\n        size_bytes,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Format bytes as human-readable size\nfn format_bytes(bytes: u64) -> String {\n    const KB: u64 = 1024;\n    const MB: u64 = 1024 * KB;\n    const GB: u64 = 1024 * MB;\n\n    if bytes >= GB {\n        format!(\"{:.1} GB\", bytes as f64 / GB as f64)\n    } else if bytes >= MB {\n        format!(\"{:.1} MB\", bytes as f64 / MB as f64)\n    } else if bytes >= KB {\n        format!(\"{:.1} KB\", bytes as f64 / KB as f64)\n    } else {\n        format!(\"{} B\", bytes)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Format a timestamp as relative time ago\nfn format_ago(ts: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>) -> String {\n    let now = chrono::Utc::now();\n    let duration = now.signed_duration_since(ts);\n\n    if duration.num_days() > 0 {\n        format!(\"{}d ago\", duration.num_days())\n    } else if duration.num_hours() > 0 {\n        format!(\"{}h ago\", duration.num_hours())\n    } else if duration.num_minutes() > 0 {\n        format!(\"{}m ago\", duration.num_minutes())\n    } else {\n        \"just now\".to_string()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Recursively compute directory size in bytes\nfn dir_size(path: &std::path::Path) -> u64 {\n    if !path.exists() {\n        return 0;\n    }\n\n    if path.is_file() {\n        return path.metadata().map(|m| m.len()).unwrap_or(0);\n    }\n\n    let mut total: u64 = 0;\n    if let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(path) {\n        for entry in entries.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n            let p = entry.path();\n            if p.is_dir() {\n                total += dir_size(&p);\n            } else if let Ok(m) = p.metadata() {\n                total += m.len();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    total\n}\n\n/// Count files with a given extension recursively\n#[allow(dead_code)]\nfn count_files_recursive(path: &std::path::Path, ext: &str) -> usize {\n    if !path.is_dir() {\n        return 0;\n    }\n\n    let mut count = 0;\n    if let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(path) {\n        for entry in entries.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n            let p = entry.path();\n            if p.is_dir() {\n                count += count_files_recursive(&p, ext);\n            } else if p.extension().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) == Some(ext) {\n                count += 1;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    count\n}\n\n/// Load configuration from default location\nfn load_config() -> Result<Config> {\n    let config_path = config::config_path();\n    if let Some(path) = config_path {\n        Config::load(&path)\n    } else {\n        Ok(Config::default())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run recurring problem detection\nfn run_recurring(since: Option<String>, threshold: usize, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let since_dt = match since {\n        Some(ref s) => search::parse_datetime(s)?,\n        None => chrono::Utc::now() - chrono::Duration::days(30),\n    };\n\n    let opts = crate::recurring::RecurringOptions {\n        since: since_dt,\n        threshold,\n    };\n\n    let output = crate::recurring::detect_recurring(&data_dir, &opts)?;\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", crate::recurring::format_human(&output));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run rules extraction command\nfn run_rules(project_path: PathBuf, format: String, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let output_format = match crate::rules::OutputFormat::from_str(&format) {\n        Some(f) => f,\n        None => {\n            eprintln!(\"Unknown format: {}. Use claude, cursor, or aider.\", format);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    let output = crate::rules::extract_rules(&data_dir, &project_path)?;\n\n    if json {\n        use serde_json::json;\n        let rules_json: Vec<serde_json::Value> = output\n            .rules\n            .iter()\n            .map(|r| match r {\n                crate::rules::Rule::Correction(s) => json!({\"type\": \"correction\", \"rule\": s}),\n                crate::rules::Rule::Convention(s) => json!({\"type\": \"convention\", \"rule\": s}),\n                crate::rules::Rule::Context(s) => json!({\"type\": \"context\", \"rule\": s}),\n                crate::rules::Rule::Warning(s) => json!({\"type\": \"warning\", \"rule\": s}),\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        let result = json!({\n            \"project_path\": output.project_path.display().to_string(),\n            \"sessions_analyzed\": output.sessions_analyzed,\n            \"rules\": rules_json,\n        });\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&result).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        if output.rules.is_empty() {\n            println!(\"{}\", crate::rules::format_human(&output));\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n\n        let path = crate::rules::write_rules(&output, output_format, &project_path)?;\n        println!(\n            \"Wrote {} rules to {} ({} sessions analyzed)\",\n            output.rules.len(),\n            path.display(),\n            output.sessions_analyzed,\n        );\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run analytics command\nfn run_analytics(\n    agent: Option<String>,\n    project: Option<String>,\n    since: Option<String>,\n    json: bool,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let since_dt = match since {\n        Some(ref s) => Some(search::parse_datetime(s)?),\n        None => None,\n    };\n\n    let opts = crate::analytics::AnalyticsOptions {\n        agent,\n        project,\n        since: since_dt,\n    };\n\n    let output = crate::analytics::compute_analytics(&data_dir, &opts, &config)?;\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", crate::analytics::format_human(&output));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run garbage collection command\nfn run_gc(older_than: Option<String>, dry_run: bool, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Determine max age: CLI arg > config > error\n    let max_age = if let Some(ref duration_str) = older_than {\n        crate::gc::parse_duration(duration_str)?\n    } else if config.scrape.max_session_age_days > 0 {\n        chrono::Duration::days(config.scrape.max_session_age_days as i64)\n    } else {\n        eprintln!(\"No max session age configured. Set scrape.max_session_age_days in config.toml or use --older-than.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    };\n\n    let result = crate::gc::run_gc(&data_dir, max_age, dry_run)?;\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&result).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", crate::gc::format_human(&result));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run blame command: show sessions associated with a file/line via git blame.\nfn run_blame(spec: String, max_results: usize, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let (file, line) = parse_blame_spec(&spec);\n\n    // If a line number was given, try to resolve the commit hash via git blame.\n    let commit_hash = if let Some(ln) = line {\n        git_blame_commit(&file, ln)\n    } else {\n        None\n    };\n\n    let opts = if let Some(hash) = commit_hash {\n        search::SearchOptions {\n            git_commit: Some(hash),\n            max_results,\n            sort: search::SortOrder::Newest,\n            ..Default::default()\n        }\n    } else {\n        search::SearchOptions {\n            file_path: Some(file.clone()),\n            max_results,\n            sort: search::SortOrder::Newest,\n            ..Default::default()\n        }\n    };\n\n    let output = match search::execute_search(&data_dir, &opts) {\n        Ok(o) => o,\n        Err(e) => {\n            eprintln!(\"Search error: {}\", e);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        if let Some(ln) = line {\n            println!(\"Sessions related to {}:{}\", file, ln);\n        } else {\n            println!(\"Sessions that touched: {}\", file);\n        }\n        println!(\"{}\", search::format_human(&output, 200));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run file command: show all sessions that touched a file, chronologically.\nfn run_file(path: String, max_results: usize, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let opts = search::SearchOptions {\n        file_path: Some(path.clone()),\n        max_results,\n        sort: search::SortOrder::Oldest,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n\n    let output = match search::execute_search(&data_dir, &opts) {\n        Ok(o) => o,\n        Err(e) => {\n            eprintln!(\"Search error: {}\", e);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        println!(\"Sessions that touched: {}\", path);\n        println!(\"{}\", search::format_human(&output, 200));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// A summary entry for a single session (used in run_summarize).\n#[derive(serde::Serialize)]\nstruct SummaryEntry {\n    session_id: String,\n    summary: String,\n    project: Option<String>,\n    started: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,\n    outcome: Option<String>,\n    files_touched: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n/// Run summarize command: generate Markdown summaries for sessions.\nfn run_summarize(\n    session: Option<String>,\n    since: Option<String>,\n    project: Option<String>,\n    max_results: usize,\n    write: bool,\n    json: bool,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n    if !sessions_dir.exists() {\n        println!(\"No sessions found. Run 'agentscribe scrape' first.\");\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    let since_dt = since.as_deref().map(search::parse_datetime).transpose()?;\n\n    let mut entries: Vec<SummaryEntry> = Vec::new();\n\n    if let Some(ref sid) = session {\n        // Specific session\n        let events = read_session_events(&sessions_dir, sid)?;\n        if events.is_empty() {\n            eprintln!(\"Session '{}' not found or has no events\", sid);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n        let agent = sid.split('/').next().unwrap_or(\"unknown\");\n        let manifest = crate::index::build_manifest_from_events(\n            &events,\n            sid,\n            agent,\n            events.first().and_then(|e| e.project.as_deref()),\n            events.first().and_then(|e| e.model.as_deref()),\n        );\n        let summary = crate::enrichment::generate_summary(&events, &manifest);\n\n        if write {\n            write_summary_file(&sessions_dir, sid, &summary, &manifest)?;\n        }\n\n        entries.push(SummaryEntry {\n            session_id: sid.clone(),\n            summary,\n            project: manifest.project,\n            started: manifest.started,\n            outcome: manifest.outcome,\n            files_touched: manifest.files_touched,\n        });\n    } else {\n        // Walk sessions directory\n        let session_ids = collect_all_session_ids(&sessions_dir);\n        let mut count = 0;\n\n        for sid in session_ids {\n            if count >= max_results {\n                break;\n            }\n\n            let events = match read_session_events(&sessions_dir, &sid) {\n                Ok(e) if !e.is_empty() => e,\n                _ => continue,\n            };\n\n            let agent = sid.split('/').next().unwrap_or(\"unknown\");\n            let manifest = crate::index::build_manifest_from_events(\n                &events,\n                &sid,\n                agent,\n                events.first().and_then(|e| e.project.as_deref()),\n                events.first().and_then(|e| e.model.as_deref()),\n            );\n\n            // Apply filters\n            if let Some(ref proj) = project {\n                if manifest.project.as_deref() != Some(proj.as_str()) {\n                    continue;\n                }\n            }\n            if let Some(since) = since_dt {\n                if manifest.started < since {\n                    continue;\n                }\n            }\n\n            let summary = crate::enrichment::generate_summary(&events, &manifest);\n\n            if write {\n                write_summary_file(&sessions_dir, &sid, &summary, &manifest)?;\n            }\n\n            entries.push(SummaryEntry {\n                session_id: sid.clone(),\n                summary,\n                project: manifest.project,\n                started: manifest.started,\n                outcome: manifest.outcome,\n                files_touched: manifest.files_touched,\n            });\n\n            count += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&entries).unwrap());\n    } else if write {\n        println!(\n            \"Wrote {} summary file(s) to {}\",\n            entries.len(),\n            sessions_dir.display()\n        );\n    } else {\n        for entry in &entries {\n            println!(\"# Session: {}\", entry.session_id);\n            println!();\n            println!(\"**Summary:** {}\", entry.summary);\n            println!();\n            if let Some(ref outcome) = entry.outcome {\n                println!(\"- **Outcome:** {}\", outcome);\n            }\n            println!(\"- **Started:** {}\", entry.started.to_rfc3339());\n            if let Some(ref proj) = entry.project {\n                println!(\"- **Project:** {}\", proj);\n            }\n            if !entry.files_touched.is_empty() {\n                let files: Vec<&str> = entry\n                    .files_touched\n                    .iter()\n                    .take(5)\n                    .map(|s| s.as_str())\n                    .collect();\n                println!(\"- **Files touched:** {}\", files.join(\", \"));\n            }\n            println!();\n            println!(\"---\");\n            println!();\n        }\n        if entries.is_empty() {\n            println!(\"No sessions found.\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Parse a blame spec: \"file.rs\" or \"file.rs:42\"\nfn parse_blame_spec(spec: &str) -> (String, Option<u32>) {\n    if let Some(colon_pos) = spec.rfind(':') {\n        let file = spec[..colon_pos].to_string();\n        let line_str = &spec[colon_pos + 1..];\n        if let Ok(line) = line_str.parse::<u32>() {\n            return (file, Some(line));\n        }\n    }\n    (spec.to_string(), None)\n}\n\n/// Run git blame to find the commit hash for a specific file/line.\n/// Returns None if git is unavailable or the line is uncommitted.\nfn git_blame_commit(file: &str, line: u32) -> Option<String> {\n    let output = std::process::Command::new(\"git\")\n        .args([\n            \"blame\",\n            \"-L\",\n            &format!(\"{},{}\", line, line),\n            \"--porcelain\",\n            file,\n        ])\n        .output()\n        .ok()?;\n\n    if !output.status.success() {\n        return None;\n    }\n\n    let stdout = String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout);\n    let hash = stdout.lines().next()?.split_whitespace().next()?;\n\n    // All-zeros means the line is not yet committed\n    if hash.chars().all(|c| c == '0') {\n        return None;\n    }\n\n    Some(hash.to_string())\n}\n\n/// Read session events from the normalized sessions directory.\nfn read_session_events(\n    sessions_dir: &std::path::Path,\n    session_id: &str,\n) -> Result<Vec<crate::event::Event>> {\n    let parts: Vec<&str> = session_id.splitn(2, '/').collect();\n    if parts.len() != 2 {\n        return Ok(Vec::new());\n    }\n    let path = sessions_dir\n        .join(parts[0])\n        .join(format!(\"{}.jsonl\", parts[1]));\n    if !path.exists() {\n        return Ok(Vec::new());\n    }\n\n    use std::io::BufRead;\n    let file = std::fs::File::open(&path)?;\n    let reader = std::io::BufReader::new(file);\n    let mut events = Vec::new();\n\n    for line in reader.lines() {\n        let l = line?;\n        if l.trim().is_empty() {\n            continue;\n        }\n        if let Ok(event) = crate::event::Event::from_jsonl(&l) {\n            events.push(event);\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(events)\n}\n\n/// Collect all session IDs by walking the sessions directory.\nfn collect_all_session_ids(sessions_dir: &std::path::Path) -> Vec<String> {\n    let mut ids = Vec::new();\n\n    let Ok(agents) = std::fs::read_dir(sessions_dir) else {\n        return ids;\n    };\n\n    for agent_entry in agents.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n        let agent_path = agent_entry.path();\n        if !agent_path.is_dir() {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let Some(agent_name) = agent_path.file_name().and_then(|n| n.to_str()) else {\n            continue;\n        };\n\n        let Ok(sessions) = std::fs::read_dir(&agent_path) else {\n            continue;\n        };\n\n        for session_entry in sessions.filter_map(|e| e.ok()) {\n            let session_path = session_entry.path();\n            if session_path.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()) != Some(\"jsonl\") {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if let Some(stem) = session_path.file_stem().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) {\n                ids.push(format!(\"{}/{}\", agent_name, stem));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    ids\n}\n\n/// Write a Markdown summary file alongside the session JSONL.\nfn write_summary_file(\n    sessions_dir: &std::path::Path,\n    session_id: &str,\n    summary: &str,\n    manifest: &crate::event::SessionManifest,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let parts: Vec<&str> = session_id.splitn(2, '/').collect();\n    if parts.len() != 2 {\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n    let md_path = sessions_dir.join(parts[0]).join(format!(\"{}.md\", parts[1]));\n\n    let mut content = format!(\"# Session: {}\\n\\n\", session_id);\n    content.push_str(&format!(\"**Summary:** {}\\n\\n\", summary));\n\n    if let Some(ref outcome) = manifest.outcome {\n        content.push_str(&format!(\"- **Outcome:** {}\\n\", outcome));\n    }\n    content.push_str(&format!(\n        \"- **Started:** {}\\n\",\n        manifest.started.to_rfc3339()\n    ));\n    if let Some(ref proj) = manifest.project {\n        content.push_str(&format!(\"- **Project:** {}\\n\", proj));\n    }\n    if !manifest.files_touched.is_empty() {\n        let files: Vec<&str> = manifest\n            .files_touched\n            .iter()\n            .take(10)\n            .map(|s| s.as_str())\n            .collect();\n        content.push_str(&format!(\"- **Files touched:** {}\\n\", files.join(\", \")));\n    }\n    content.push('\\n');\n\n    std::fs::write(&md_path, content)?;\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run file knowledge command\nfn run_file_knowledge(file_path: &str, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let knowledge = crate::file_knowledge::build_file_knowledge(&data_dir, file_path, &config)?;\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&knowledge).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", crate::file_knowledge::format_human(&knowledge));\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run pulse-report command\nfn run_pulse_report(quarter: String, output: Option<String>, format: String) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let fmt = match crate::pulse_report::ReportFormat::parse(&format) {\n        Some(f) => f,\n        None => {\n            eprintln!(\"Unknown format '{}'. Use markdown, html, or json.\", format);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    let opts = crate::pulse_report::PulseReportOptions {\n        quarter: quarter.clone(),\n        output: output.clone(),\n        format: fmt,\n    };\n\n    let report = crate::pulse_report::generate_pulse_report(&data_dir, &opts, &config)?;\n\n    let content = match fmt {\n        crate::pulse_report::ReportFormat::Markdown => {\n            crate::pulse_report::format_markdown(&report)\n        }\n        crate::pulse_report::ReportFormat::Html => crate::pulse_report::format_html(&report),\n        crate::pulse_report::ReportFormat::Json => crate::pulse_report::format_json(&report),\n    };\n\n    if let Some(ref path) = output {\n        std::fs::write(path, &content)?;\n        eprintln!(\"Pulse Report ({}) written to {}\", report.quarter, path);\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", content);\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run capacity command\nfn run_capacity(account_dirs: Vec<PathBuf>, cache_max_age: u64, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    use crate::capacity::{CapacityMeter, CapacityMeterConfig};\n\n    let config = if account_dirs.is_empty() {\n        CapacityMeterConfig::default()\n    } else {\n        CapacityMeterConfig {\n            account_dirs,\n            cache_max_age_secs: cache_max_age,\n            cache_base_dir: None,\n        }\n    };\n\n    let meter = CapacityMeter::new(config);\n    let accounts = meter.compute();\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&accounts).unwrap());\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    if accounts.is_empty() {\n        println!(\"No Claude accounts found.\");\n        println!(\"Expected: ~/.claude/.credentials.json (or ~/.claude-*/.credentials.json)\");\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    println!(\"Claude Code Capacity\\n\");\n\n    for acct in &accounts {\n        println!(\n            \"Account: {} ({} / {})\",\n            acct.account_id, acct.plan_type, acct.rate_limit_tier\n        );\n        println!(\"  Source: {}\", acct.source);\n\n        let bar_5h = util_bar(acct.utilization_5h);\n        let reset_5h = acct\n            .resets_at_5h\n            .map(|dt| format!(\"  resets {}\", format_resets_at(dt)))\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n
