acct\n            .resets_at_7d\n            .map(|dt| format!(\"  resets {}\", format_resets_at(dt)))\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n        println!(\n            \"  7d window:  {:5.1}%  {}{}\",\n            acct.utilization_7d, bar_7d, reset_7d\n        );\n\n        if !acct.model_windows_7d.is_empty() {\n            for mw in &acct.model_windows_7d {\n                let bar = util_bar(mw.utilization);\n                println!(\"    {:10} {:5.1}%  {}\", mw.model, mw.utilization, bar);\n            }\n        }\n\n        if acct.burn_rate_per_min > 0.0 {\n            println!(\"  Burn rate:  {:.0} tokens/min\", acct.burn_rate_per_min);\n            if let Some(mins) = acct.forecast_full_5h_min {\n                if mins > 0.0 {\n                    println!(\" println!(\n            \"  Turns:      {} (5h)  {} (7d)\",\n            acct.turns_5h, acct.turns_7d\n        );\n        println!();\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\nfn util_bar(util: f64) -> String {\n    let filled = ((util / 100.0) * 20.0).round() as usize;\n    let filled = filled.min(20);\n    let empty = 20 - filled;\n    format!(\"[{}{}]\", \"█\".repeat(filled), \"░\".repeat(empty))\n}\n\nfn format_resets_at(dt: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>) -> String {\n    use chrono::Utc;\n    let now = Utc::now();\n    let delta = dt - now;\n    let total_secs = delta.num_seconds();\n    if total_secs <= 0 {\n        return \"now\".to_string();\n    }\n    let hours = total_secs / 3600;\n    let mins = (total_secs % 3600) / 60;\n    if hours > 0 {\n        format!(\"in {}h {}m\", hours, mins)\n    } else {\n        format!(\"in {}m\", mins)\n    }\n}\n\nfn format_minutes(mins: f64) -> String {\n    if mins < 60.0 {\n        format!(\"{:.0}m\", mins)\n    } else {\n        format!(\"{:.1}h\", mins / 60.0)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run transcribe command\nfn run_transcribe(input: PathBuf, wait: bool, timeout: u64, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n\n    if !config.whisper.enabled {\n        eprintln!(\n            \"Whisper transcription is disabled.\\n\\\n             Enable it in config.toml:\\n\\n\\\n             [whisper]\\n\\\n             enabled = true\\n\\\n             model_path = \\\"~/.agentscribe/models/ggml-base.bin\\\"\\n\\\n             backend = \\\"whisper_cpp\\\"\"\n        );\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    if !input.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"File not found: {}\", input.display());\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let rt = tokio::runtime::Runtime::new().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::Transcription(format!(\n            \"failed to create async runtime: {}\",\n            e\n        ))\n    })?;\n\n    // For fire-and-forget (--no-wait), submit to the queue and print job ID.\n    if !wait {\n        let job_id = rt.block_on(async {\n            let queue = crate::transcription::TranscriptionQueue::new(\n                config.whisper.clone(),\n                config.redaction.clone(),\n            );\n            queue.submit(input, config.whisper.max_retries).await\n        })?;\n        println!(\"Transcription job submitted: {}\", job_id);\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    // Synchronous path: run transcription and wait for the result.\n    let job = rt.block_on(async {\n        let queue = crate::transcription::TranscriptionQueue::new(\n            config.whisper.clone(),\n            config.redaction.clone(),\n        );\n        let job_id = queue.submit(input, config.whisper.max_retries).await?;\n        queue\n            .wait_for_job(&job_id, std::time::Duration::from_secs(timeout))\n            .await\n    })?;\n\n    let result = match job.result {\n        Some(r) => r,\n        None => {\n            eprintln!(\n                \"Transcription failed: {}\",\n                job.error.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"unknown error\")\n            );\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    // ── Output ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    if json {\n        println!(\n            \"{}\",\n            serde_json::to_string_pretty(&result).map_err(|e| {\n                crate::error::AgentScribeError::Transcription(format!(\n                    \"JSON serialization failed: {}\",\n                    e\n                ))\n            })?\n        );\n    } else {\n        // Warning card for degraded results.\n        if result.has_warnings {\n            eprintln!(\"┌─ TRANSCRIPTION WARNINGS ─────────────────────────────────────┐\");\n            for w in &result.warnings {\n                eprintln!(\"│  {}\", w);\n            }\n            eprintln!(\"└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\");\n        }\n\n        println!(\"{}\", result.full_text);\n\n        // Summary line with timestamp granularity info.\n        let level = match result.timestamp_level {\n            crate::transcription::TimestampLevel::Word => \"word-level\",\n            crate::transcription::TimestampLevel::Utterance => \"utterance-level (fallback)\",\n        };\n        eprintln!(\n            \"[{} segments, {}, transcribed at {}]\",\n            result.segment_count(),\n            level,\n            result.transcribed_at.to_rfc3339(),\n        );\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run digest command\nfn run_digest(since: String, output: Option<String>, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let since_dt = search::parse_datetime(&since)?;\n\n    let opts = crate::digest::DigestOptions {\n        since: since_dt,\n        output: output.clone(),\n        json,\n    };\n\n    let digest_output = crate::digest::generate_digest(&data_dir, &opts, &config)?;\n\n    let content = if json {\n        crate::digest::format_json(&digest_output)\n    } else {\n        crate::digest::format_markdown(&digest_output)\n    };\n\n    if let Some(path) = output {\n        std::fs::write(&path, &content)?;\n        eprintln!(\"Digest written to {}\", path);\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", content);\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run context command: pre-task priming query for agent workers\nfn run_context(\n    query: String,\n    token_budget: usize,\n    project: Option<PathBuf>,\n    json: bool,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Store the current_dir in a variable to avoid lifetime issues\n    let current_dir = std::env::current_dir().ok();\n    let project_path = if let Some(ref p) = project {\n        Some(p.as_path())\n    } else {\n        current_dir.as_deref()\n    };\n\n    let pack = crate::search::context_pack(&data_dir, &query, token_budget, project_path)?;\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&pack).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", pack.format_text());\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run render command: export a session as HTML or Markdown\nfn run_render(session_id: String, output: Option<PathBuf>, format: String) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n    if !sessions_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"No sessions directory found. Run 'agentscribe scrape' first.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Parse session ID to get agent and session parts\n    let parts: Vec<&str> = session_id.splitn(2, '/').collect();\n    if parts.len() != 2 {\n        eprintln!(\"Invalid session ID format. Use 'html' or 'markdown'.\", format);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Output to file or stdout\n    if let Some(path) = output {\n        std::fs::write(&path, &content)?;\n        eprintln!(\"Rendered session '{}' to {}\", session_id, path.display());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", content);\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n","numLines":2761,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2761}}}

Ok(html)\n117\t}\n118\t\n119\t/// Render a session as structured Markdown\n120\tpub fn render_markdown(events: &[Event], meta: &SessionManifest) -> Result<String> {\n121\t    let mut md = String::new();\n122\t\n123\t    // YAML frontmatter\n124\t    md.push_str(\"---\\n\");\n125\t    md.push_str(&format!(\"session_id: {}\\n\", meta.session_id));\n126\t    md.push_str(&format!(\"source_agent: {}\\n\", meta.source_agent));\n127\t    if let Some(ref project) = meta.project {\n128\t        md.push_str(&format!(\"project: {}\\n\", project));\n129\t    }\n130\t    md.push_str(&format!(\"started: {}\\n\", meta.started.to_rfc3339()));\n131\t    if let Some(ref ended) = meta.ended {\n132\t        md.push_str(&format!(\"ended: {}\\n\", {}\\n\", outcome));\n137\t    }\n138\t    if !meta.files_touched.is_empty() {\n139\t        md.push_str(\"files_touched:\\n\");\n140\t        for file in &meta.files_touched {\n141\t            md.push_str(&format!(\"  - {}\\n\", file));\n142\t        }\n143\t    }\n144\t    if let Some(ref model) = meta.model {\n145\t        md.push_str(&format!(\"model: {}\\n\", model));\n146\t    }\n147\t    md.push_str(\"---\\n\\n\");\n148\t\n149\t    // Summary if available\n150\t    if let Some(ref summary) = meta.summary {\n151\t        md.push_str(&format!(\"**Summary:** {}\\n\\n\", summary));\n152\t    }\n153\t\n154\t    // Conversation\n155\t    for event in events {\n156\t        let role_label = match event.role {\n157\t            Role::User => \"**User**\",\n158\t ));\n169\t\n170\t        if let Some(ref tool) = event.tool {\n171\t            md.push_str(&format!(\"*Tool: {}*\\n\\n\", tool));\n172\t        }\n173\t\n174\t        // Render content with code Render content with code block detection for HTML\n183\tfn render_content_html(content: &str) -> String {\n184\t    let mut result = String::new();\n185\t    let mut pos = 0;\n186\t\n187\t    // Detect code blocks: ```lang ... ```\n188\t    while let Some(fence_start) = content[pos..].find(\"```\") {\n189\t        // Add text before fence\n190\t        let before_fence = &content[pos..pos + fence_start];\n191\t        result.push_str(&escape_html(before_fence));\n192\t\n193\t        pos += fence_start + 3;\n194\t\n195\t        // Extract language (rest of line)\n196\t        let lang_end = content[pos..].find('\\n').unwrap_or(content[pos..].len());\n197\t        let lang = &content[pos..pos + lang_end];\n198\t        let lang = lang.trim();\n199\t\n200\t        pos += lang_end + 1; // Skip newline\n201\t\n202\t        // Find closing fence\n203\t        if let Some(fence_end) = content[pos..].find(\"```\") {\n204\t            let code = &content[pos..pos + fence_end];\n205\t\n206\t            result.push_str(\"<pre><code class=\\\"language-\");\n207\t            result.push_str(&escape_html(lang));\n208\t            result.push_str(\"\\\">\");\n209\t            result.push_str(&escape_html(code));\n210\t            result.push_str(\"</code></pre>\");\n211\t\n212\t            pos += fence_end + 3;\n213\t\n214\t            // Skip trailing newline\n215\t            if pos < content.len() && content.as_bytes()[pos] == b'\\n' {\n216\t                pos += 1;\n217\t            }\n218\t        } else {\n219\t            // No closing fence, treat rest as text\n220\t            result.push_str(\"<pre>\");\n221\t            result.push_str(&escape_html(&content[pos..]));\n222\t            result.push_str(\"</pre>\");\n223\t            break;\n224\t        }\n225\t    }\n226\t\n227\t    // Add remaining text\n228\t    if pos < content.len() {\n229\t        result.push_str(&escape_html(&content[pos..]));\n230\t    }\n231\t\n232\t    result\n233\t}\n234\t\n235\t/// Render content with code block detection for Markdown\n236\tfn render_content_markdown(content: &str) -> String {\n237\t    // For Markdown, we mostly preserve the original formatting\n238\t    // Just ensure newlines are handled correctly\n239\t    content.to_string()\n240\t}\n241\t\n242\t/// Format duration between start and end\n243\tfn format_duration(start: DateTime<Utc>, end: Option<DateTime<Utc>>) -> String {\n244\t    let end = end.unwrap_or_else(Utc::now);\n245\t    let duration = end.signed_duration_since(start);\n246\t\n247\t    let mut parts: Vec<String> = Vec::new();\n248\t\n249\t    if duration.num_days() > 0 {\n250\t        parts.push(format!(\"{}d\", duration.num_days()));\n251\t    }\n252\t    if duration.num_hours() % 24 > 0 {\n253\t        parts.push(format!(\"{}h\", duration.num_hours() % 24));\n254\t    }\n255\t    if duration.num_minutes() % 60 > 0 {\n256\t        parts.push(format!(\"{}m\", duration.num_minutes() % 60));\n257\t    }\n258\t\n259\t    if parts.is_empty() {\n260\t        \"<1m\".to_string()\n261\t    } else {\n262\t        parts.join(\" \")\n263\t    }\n264\t}\n265\t\n266\t/// Format model(s) used\n267\tfn format_models(model: Option<&str>) -> String {\n268\t    model.unwrap_or(\"unknown\").to_string()\n269\t}\n270\t\n271\t/// Format timestamp for display\n272\tfn format_timestamp(ts: &DateTime<Utc>) -> String {\n273\t    ts.format(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC\").to_string()\n274\t}\n275\t\n276\t/// Get role badge label\n277\tfn role_badge_label(role: &Role) -> &'static str {\n278\t    match role {\n279\t        Role::User => \"User\",\n280\t        Role::Assistant => \"Assistant\",\n281\t        Role::System => \"System\",\n282\t        Role::ToolCall => \"Tool\",\n283\t        Role::ToolResult => \"Result\",\n284\t    }\n285\t}\n286\t\n287\t/// Escape HTML special characters\n288\tfn escape_html(s: &str) -> String {\n289\t    let mut result = String::with_capacity(s.len());\n290\t    for c in s.chars() {\n291\t        match c {\n292\t            '&' => result.push_str(\"&amp;\"),\n293\t            '<' => result.push_str(\"&lt;\"),\n294\t            '>' => result.push_str(\"&gt;\"),\n295\t            '\"' => result.push_str(\"&quot;\"),\n296\t            '\\'' => result.push_str(\"&#x27;\"),\n297\t            c => result.push(c),\n298\t        }\n299\t    }\n300\t    result\n301\t}\n302\t\n303\t/// Inline CSS for HTML output (~3KB budget)\n304\tconst CSS: &str = r#\"\n305\t:root {\n306\t  --bg: #ffffff;\n307\t  --fg: #1a1a1a;\n308\t }\n534\t\n535\t    #[test]\n536\t    fn test_escape_html() {\n537\t        assert_eq!(escape_html(\"<script>\"), \"&lt;script&gt;\");\n538\t        assert_eq!(escape_html(\"a & b\"), \"a &amp; Render a session as structured Markdown\npub fn render_markdown(events: &[Event], meta: &SessionManifest) -> Result<String> {\n    let mut md = String::new();\n\n    // YAML frontmatter\n blocks: ```lang ... ```\n    while let Some(fence_start) = content[pos..].find(\"```\") {\n        // Add text before fence\n        let before_fence = &content[pos..pos + fence_start];\n result.push_str(&escape_html(&content[pos..]));\n            result.push_str(\"</pre>\");\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Add remaining text\n    if pos < content.len() {\n        result.push_str(&escape_html(&content[pos..]));\n    }\n\n    result\n}\n\n/// Render content with code block detection for Markdown\nfn render_content_markdown(content: &str) -> String {\n    // For
